focus_tree = {

	id = usa_focus
	
	country = {
		factor = 0
		
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			tag = USA
		}

		modifier = {
			add = 10
			original_tag = USA
		}
	}

	default = no

	continuous_focus_position = { x = 10 y = 10000 }

	id = WILSON_USA_ill_presidency

	cost = 1

	x = 0
	y = 0
	
	available_if_capitulated =  no

		NOT = {
			has_flag = USA_state_of_emergency
		}
	}

	completion_reward = {
		country_event = {
			id = usaWilson.1
		}
	}
}

#Wilson Demobilization#

focus = {
	id = WILSON_USA_begin_demobilization
	icon = GFX_focus_USA_placeholder

	cost = 4

	x = 3
	y = 1
	
	prerequisite = { focus = EXTRA_WILSON_USA_crack_down_on_poor_industry_practices }
	relative_position_id = EXTRA_WILSON_USA_crack_down_on_poor_industry_practices



	available_if_capitulated = no		

	available = {
		NOT = {
			has_flag = USA_state_of_emergency
		}
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = bloated_army #demobing too fast can destroy economy and unlocks decisions to begin getting rid of massive_army idea
		custom_effect_tooltip = demob_warning_tt
	}
}

focus = {
	id = WILSON_USA_cut_industrial_budget
	icon = GFX_focus_USA_placeholder

	cost = 4

	x = 0
	y = 1
	
	prerequisite = { focus = EXTRA_WILSON_USA_innaugaration_speech }
	relative_position_id = EXTRA_WILSON_USA_innaugaration_speech



	available_if_capitulated = no		

	available = {
		NOT = {
			has_flag = USA_state_of_emergency
		}
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		add_to_variable = { bloated_military_expenditures_factor_var = -0.3 }
		add_to_variable = { bloated_industrial_capacity_factory_var = -0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { bloated_industrial_capacity_dockyard_var = -0.1 }
	}
}

focus = {
	id = WILSON_USA_veteran_bonus_check
	icon = GFX_focus_USA_placeholder

	cost = 4

	x = 0
	y = 3
	
	prerequisite = { focus = WILSON_USA_begin_demobilization }
	relative_position_id = WILSON_USA_begin_demobilization



	available_if_capitulated = no		

	available = {
		NOT = {
			has_flag = USA_state_of_emergency
		}
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		add_to_variable = { gdp_roaring_growth_var = 0.01 }
		add_to_variable = { political_roaring__var = 0.03 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = GDP }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.08 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { bloated_military_expenditures_factor_var = 0.25 }
		}
	}
}

focus = {
	id = WILSON_USA_threathen_senators
	icon = GFX_focus_USA_placeholder

	cost = 4

	x = -1
	y = 1
	
	prerequisite = { focus = WILSON_USA_rights_of_man }
	relative_position_id = WILSON_USA_rights_of_man

	mutually_exclusive = { focus = WILSON_USA_compromise_with_conservatives }

	available = {
		always = no
	}

	available_if_capitulated = no		

	available = {
		NOT = {
			has_flag = USA_state_of_emergency
		}
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.1
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -30 
		#splits the party and weakens chance for wilson & party to win southern victory
	}
}

focus = {
	id = FDR_USA_puerto_rico_relief_administration
	icon = GFX_focus_USA_placeholder

	cost = 1

	x = 0
	y = 2
	
	prerequisite = { focus = FDR_USA_three_rs }
	relative_position_id = FDR_USA_three_rs

	available_if_capitulated = no		

	available = {
		NOT = {
			has_flag = USA_state_of_emergency
		}
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		597 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.1 }
			econ_state_value_change_multiply_specified_state = yes
			add_state_modifier = {
				modifier = {
					state_GDP_growth_factor_modifier = 0.10
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
